id=\"openlineage-client-uuid-module\"></span><h2>openlineage.client.uuid module</h2>\n<dl class=\"py function\">\n<dt class=\"sig sig-object py\" id=\"openlineage.client.uuid.generate_new_uuid\">\n<span class=\"sig-prename descclassname\"><span class=\"pre\">openlineage.client.uuid.</span></span><span class=\"sig-name descname\"><span class=\"pre\">generate_new_uuid</span></span><span class=\"sig-paren\">(</span><em class=\"sig-param\"><span class=\"n\"><span class=\"pre\">instant</span></span><span class=\"o\"><span class=\"pre\">=</span></span><span class=\"default_value\"><span class=\"pre\">None</span></span></em><span class=\"sig-paren\">)</span></dt>\n<dd><p>Generate new UUID for an instant of time. Each function call returns a new UUID value.</p>\n<p>UUID version is an implementation detail, and <strong>should not</strong> be relied on.\nFor now it is [UUIDv7](<a class=\"reference external\" href=\"https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9562/\">https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9562/</a>), so for increasing instant values,\nreturned UUID is always greater than previous one.</p>\n<p>Using uuid6 lib implementation (MIT License), with few changes:\n* <a class=\"github reference external\" href=\"https://github.com/oittaa/uuid6-python/blob/4f879849178b8a7a564f7cb76c3f7a6e5228d9ed/src/uuid6/__init__.py#L128-L147\">oittaa/uuid6-python</a>\n* <a class=\"github reference external\" href=\"https://github.com/oittaa/uuid6-python/blob/4f879849178b8a7a564f7cb76c3f7a6e5228d9ed/src/uuid6/__init__.py#L46-L51\">oittaa/uuid6-python</a></p>\n<p>Added in v1.15.0</p>\n<dl class=\"field-list simple\">\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Parameters<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-odd\"><p><strong>instant</strong> (<span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\">datetime | None</span>) \u2013 instant of time used to generate UUID. If not provided, current time is used.</p>\n</dd>\n<dt class=\"field-even\">Return type<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-even\"><p><span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\">UUID</span></p>\n</dd>\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Returns<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-odd\"><p>UUID</p>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n</dd></dl>\n<dl class=\"py function\">\n<dt class=\"sig sig-object py\" id=\"openlineage.client.uuid.generate_static_uuid\">\n<span class=\"sig-prename descclassname\"><span class=\"pre\">openlineage.client.uuid.</span></span><span class=\"sig-name descname\"><span class=\"pre\">generate_static_uuid</span></span><span class=\"sig-paren\">(</span><em class=\"sig-param\"><span class=\"n\"><span class=\"pre\">instant</span></span></em>, <em class=\"sig-param\"><span class=\"n\"><span class=\"pre\">data</span></span></em><span class=\"sig-paren\">)</span></dt>\n<dd><p>Generate UUID for instant of time and input data.\nCalling function with same arguments always produces the same result.</p>\n<p>UUID version is an implementation detail, and <a href=\"#id1\"><span class=\"problematic\" id=\"id2\">**</span></a>should not* be relied on.\nFor now it is [UUIDv7](<a class=\"reference external\" href=\"https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9562/\">https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9562/</a>), so for increasing instant values,\nreturned UUID is always greater than previous one. The only difference from RFC 9562 is that\nleast significant bytes are not random, but instead a SHA-1 hash of input data.</p>\n<p>Using uuid6 lib implementation (MIT License), with few changes:\n* <a class=\"github reference external\" href=\"https://github.com/oittaa/uuid6-python/blob/4f879849178b8a7a564f7cb76c3f7a6e5228d9ed/src/uuid6/__init__.py#L128-L147\">oittaa/uuid6-python</a>\n* <a class=\"github reference external\" href=\"https://github.com/oittaa/uuid6-python/blob/4f879849178b8a7a564f7cb76c3f7a6e5228d9ed/src/uuid6/__init__.py#L46-L51\">oittaa/uuid6-python</a></p>\n<p>Added in v1.15.0</p>\n<dl class=\"field-list simple\">\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Parameters<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-odd\"><ul class=\"simple\">\n<li><p><strong>instant</strong> (<span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\"><code class=\"xref py py-class docutils literal notranslate\"><span class=\"pre\">datetime</span></code></span>) \u2013 instant of time used to generate UUID. If not provided, current time is used.</p></li>\n<li><p><strong>data</strong> (<span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\"><code class=\"xref py py-class docutils literal notranslate\"><span class=\"pre\">bytes</span></code></span>) \u2013 input data to generate random part from.</p></li>\n</ul>\n</dd>\n<dt class=\"field-even\">Return type<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-even\"><p><span class=\"sphinx_autodoc_typehints-type\"><code class=\"xref py py-class docutils literal notranslate\"><span class=\"pre\">UUID</span></code></span></p>\n</dd>\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Returns<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-odd\"><p>UUID</p>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n</dd></dl>\n</section>\n<section id=\"module-openlineage.client.generated.base\">\n<span id=\"openlineage-client-generated-base-module\"></span><h2>openlineage.client.generated.base module</h2>\n<dl class=\"py function\">\n<dt id=\"openlineage-client-transport-transport-module\"></span><h2>openlineage.client.transport.transport module</h2>\n<p>To implement custom Transport implement Config and Transport classes.</p>\n<dl class=\"simple\">\n<dt>Transport needs to</dt><dd><ul class=\"simple\">\n<li><p>specify class variable <cite>config</cite> that will point to Config class that Transport requires</p></li>\n<li><p>__init__ that will accept specified Config class instance</p></li>\n<li><p>implement <cite>emit</cite> method that will accept RunEvent</p></li>\n</ul>\n</dd>\n</dl>\n<p>Config file is read and parameters there are passed to <cite>from_dict</cite> classmethod.\nThe config class can have more complex attributes, but needs to be able to\ninstantiate them in <cite>from_dict</cite> method.</p>\n<p>DefaultTransportFactory instantiates custom transports by looking at <cite>type</cite> field in\nclass config.</p>\n<dl class=\"py class\">\n<dt class=\"sig sig-object py\" id=\"openlineage.client.transport.transport.Config\">\n<em class=\"property\"><span class=\"pre\">class</span><span class=\"w\"> </span></em><span class=\"pre\">Config</span></span></dt>\n<dd><p>Bases: <code class=\"xref py py-class docutils literal notranslate\"><span class=\"pre\">object</span></code></p>\n<dl class=\"py method\">\n<dt class=\"sig sig-object py\" id=\"openlineage.client.transport.transport.Config.from_dict\">\n<em class=\"property\"><span class=\"pre\">classmethod</span><span class=\"w\"> </span></em><span class=\"sig-paren\">)</span></dt>\n<dd><dl class=\"field-list simple\">\n<dt class=\"field-odd\">Parameters<span class=\"colon\">:</span></dt>\n<dd class=\"field-odd\"><p><strong>params</strong>
